class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baard.html>baard</a> (4251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baert</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bart.html>bart</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:bard.html>bard</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bardaz</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰardʰ-eh₂</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a> (550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baes</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:master.html>master</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> household, <a href = vnd.unilang:friend.html>friend</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*baso</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:uncle.html>uncle</a>, kinsman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baswô</i>. <ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:boss.html>boss</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:chief.html>chief</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:superior.html>superior</a></li>

***backgammon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a> (32057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>Probably</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:back.html>back</a></i> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamen.html>gamen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:gamen.html>gamen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:amusement.html>amusement</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:game.html>game</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/150px-Backgammon_lg.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="100" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/225px-Backgammon_lg.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Backgammon_lg.jpg/300px-Backgammon_lg.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:backgammon.html>backgammon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:board.html>board</a> shown <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> starting <a href = vnd.unilang:position.html>position</a>.</div></div></div>
